 ศอออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออสออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ณ  Dear Reader :                                                             ณ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ณ      We're baaaaaaack!!!  The editors of Reality Check Network took a      ณ
 ณ  short break about 3 months ago, but we've decided that the scene          ณ
 ณ  currently lacks a comprehensive magazine to inform the warez public of    ณ
 ณ  new things that occur.  So, we're back, and better than ever!!!           ณ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ณ      There are a number of new things in this issue.  First of all, part   ณ
 ณ  of the coding has been redone, so RCN has a new look.  Next, we now have  ณ
 ณ  a pop-up options menu that can be activated from anywhere in the          ณ
 ณ  magazine, so if you're in the middle of reading an article and want to    ณ
 ณ  change something (such as the music volume) you can do so without         ณ
 ณ  exiting the article first.  This issue also contains a "secret article."  ณ
 ณ  Well no, it's not completely secret, but to read it, you'll need a        ณ
 ณ  password, and to get that password, you'll have to beat the built-in      ณ
 ณ  game!  Good luck!                                                         ณ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ณ      As always, we value your opinion.  Improvements are constantly being  ณ
 ณ  made as a direct result of user input.  If you would like to participate  ณ
 ณ  in the further enhancement of RCN, or would like to send a letter to the  ณ
 ณ  editors (or to a writer in particular) please send e-mail to              ณ
 ณ  an385786@anon.penet.fi.  Note that we are no longer accepting             ณ
 ณ  subscribers to the magazine.  The reason is that the anon.penet.fi        ณ
 ณ  server will not let us send attached files over 100k in size unless we    ณ
 ณ  split them up, and that would be confusing for both us and the readers.   ณ
 ณ  To make up for that, we offer a WWW site accessible via the Internet.     ณ
 ณ  All issues will be promptly posted there.  For more information, read     ณ
 ณ  on.                                                                       ณ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ณ      In an effort to better interact with our readers, the editors of      ณ
 ณ  RCN have devised a reader survey, and would appreciate it if you would    ณ
 ณ  take the time to respond to it.  After completion of the survey, you      ณ
 ณ  simply need to send it attached to the above e-mail address.  Note that   ณ
 ณ  we prefer NOT getting messages encoded in MIME format.  We also have a    ณ
 ณ  voting booth so the readers can give input on their favorite groups.      ณ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ณ      New this issue are some little twirks that might sizzle your buns!    ณ
 ณ  For those of you that feel more confortable holding a mouse, we now have  ณ
 ณ  mouse support!  Oh, and for those of you that want to take RCN with you   ณ
 ณ  wherever you go, you can now print articles and/or the entire mag (if     ณ
 ณ  you're really cray-zee).  Oh, and if you hate that rotating music that    ณ
 ณ  we added last issue, you can turn it on and off in the Options menu.      ณ
 ณ  Note that it defaults to off.  We also have a new music track care of     ณ
 ณ  Reality, the best Adlib composing team around!                            ณ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ณ      Don't forget to keep sending in your votes for the groups you feel    ณ
 ณ  are #1, and test your wits of the scene in our Warez-IQ questionnaire,    ณ
 ณ  10 new questions in this issue!  We still have an ASCII version of the    ณ
 ณ  mag for those of you running UNIX/Linux, or those of you that want to     ณ
 ณ  save credits on your boards and view the RCN-??.TXT file in a ZIP <g>.    ณ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ณ      RCN issues have now been made available to a wider audience thanks    ณ
 ณ  to our new WebSite courtesy of RATM.  Please feel free to browse around   ณ
 ณ  - http://www.shu.edu/~importmi/rcn/.  RCN ardently feels that our         ณ
 ณ  WebSite will satisfy our readers and is a welcome addition to our         ณ
 ณ  methods of distribution.                                                  ณ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ณ      Celestian, the RCN ANSi art coordinator, will no longer be accepting  ณ
 ณ  any requests for ANSi artwork outside of RCN.  Between his artwork for    ณ
 ณ  RCN and DMN, he can longer find time to do any freelance artwork.  He     ณ
 ณ  has been receiving requests nonstop and would like to have a little       ณ
 ณ  peace here and then.                                                      ณ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ณ                                               Signed,                      ณ
 ณ                                                  Hitex/Rebel Chicken       ณ
 ณ                                                  RCN Editors               ณ
 ณ                                                                            ณ
 ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I see an obvious bias in the RCN reviews against DOD in favor of      บ
 บ  higher scores toward PWA, and it sickens me.  I think your magazine is    บ
 บ  STUPID for doing this, and hope that you will soon understand how         บ
 บ  kick-ass DOD is and how shitty PWA is.  Thank you.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  <Undisclosed>             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Your ratings of PWA are waaay too low.  You're not giving an awesome  บ
 บ  group credit for its awesome work.  DOD, on the other hand, consistently  บ
 บ  gets a higher average per release when they only release once a month.    บ
 บ  That's complete bullshit and unfair to the guys in PWA.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  <Undisclosed>             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Readers,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Alright, this is the last time (until next time) that we're going to  บ
 บ  post any messages about us being biased.  We intentionally dropped        บ
 บ  Legacy when we started up RCN again for the sole purpose of keeping an    บ
 บ  unbiased position when writing.  We have absolutely no reason to be       บ
 บ  biased towards or against anybody, and any mail that you might send us    บ
 บ  regarding the matter will be used purely for the purpose of a good        บ
 บ  laugh.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now as for my opinions on PWA vs. DOD, I think DOD has better         บ
 บ  quality, and PWA has more releases.  However, that is just a reflection   บ
 บ  of the past four weeks and is in NO WAY a consistent view of the groups.  บ
 บ  My opinion of the groups fluctuates weekly.  One week, PWA does better,   บ
 บ  the next week DOD does better.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hitex/Rebel Chicken       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I'm a member of Razor 1911 and I've been reading your E-Zine and I    บ
 บ  think it's great.  LOTS of articles that keep you reading for a long      บ
 บ  time.  Now, I have a gripe.  In your Warez-IQ test, question #4 states,   บ
 บ  "What group is known for releasing FLOPPY games?"  You only desired one   บ
 บ  answer, but Eclipse and Razor 1911 are the best candidates.  Now I know   บ
 บ  you wanted people to choose Eclipse, but the thing is, Eclipse hasn't     บ
 บ  released a floppy in MONTHS!  Razor 1911 on the other hand, has released  บ
 บ  a handful (probably two in the last week alone).                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Also, Tyranny is releasing floppy games as well, as they are one of   บ
 บ  the old school floppy game releasers (not saying the old Tyranny floppy   บ
 บ  releases were quality, but at least they were floppy).                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Toast                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Toast,                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Thank you for your response!  You make a good point in revealing      บ
 บ  that some CD-RIP game groups do a better job of releasing floppy games    บ
 บ  than some floppy-only game groups.  However, our question desired a       บ
 บ  response regarding a games group that releases nothing but floppy games,  บ
 บ  no CD-RIPs whatsoever, and Eclipse is the only one on that list.          บ
 บ  Tyranny has recently moved to CD-RIPs as well, and Razor 1911 (I don't    บ
 บ  distinguish Razor 1911 from Razor-CD), though an awesome group, is also   บ
 บ  participating in the CD-RIP scene.  Eclipse was the only choice in the    บ
 บ  list that releases only floppy games.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hitex/Rebel Chicken       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ      I have gotten a multitude of offers similar to yours this week, so I  บ
 บ  am really responding to all that wrote me.  Our current WWW site is the   บ
 บ  only "official" RCN site.  However, we will not dispute any other sites   บ
 บ  that people create for our benefit.  RATM is doing a fantastic job        บ
 บ  coordinating our current site and we feel that he is doing as good a job  บ
 บ  as anyone else could do, if not far better.  However, RATM is a busy      บ
 บ  man, and we don't want to overload him with other sites for him to        บ
 บ  update.  So, I make the request of you : if you would like to put up a    บ
 บ  WWW site containing some or all of RCN's issues, we will welcome the      บ
 บ  offer.  However, it will be up to you to update the site weekly, and      บ
 บ  keep it up to par.  We will, in support of your site, advertise it in     บ
 บ  future issues of RCN (assuming you notify us of your work).               บ

 บ      Dear RCN,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I have noticed lately that PCBoard PPEs are all looking the same      บ
 บ  with only a few mods in the ansi's or strings.  It's time for some of     บ
 บ  you BBS modders to go out and start making Renegade or Iniquity mods.     บ
 บ  PCBoard is getting old fast.  It's file system is second to none (mostly  บ
 บ  due to Boom Lab), but its message system is weak.  If there exists a new  บ
 บ  system that has the file system of PCBoard with the message bases of      บ
 บ  Renegade and Oblivion 2, can exist, modders should start to support it.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Iniquity is a nice looking BBS system.  Once it gets its bugs with    บ
 บ  blind uploads and networking/multinode out of the way it will be a kick   บ
 บ  ass system.  PPE coders should start to look at other systems since just  บ
 บ  about every PPE that could possibly be done is already made.  The reason  บ
 บ  that PCBoard is so popular is that there are so many mods for it out on   บ
 บ  the boards.  Coders should start making new Renegade and Iniquity mods    บ
 บ  that take all the strengths of PCBoard and give it to those systems.      บ
 บ  Boards that use PCBoard are beginning to look all the same with all the   บ
 บ  same or similar mods.  There is a need for Renegade and Ininuqity         บ
 บ  modders who can make quality mods.  Some of you coders should start       บ
 บ  cranking them out.  ACiD used to be the only group that had a Renegade    บ
 บ  and Iniquity support section.  It would be cool if some warez groups      บ
 บ  started to recruit some artists and coders and put them to work making    บ
 บ  practical.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Skeelo Blow               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  Dear Skeelo Blow,                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I used to be a Renegade freak.   I still think it's by far the most   บ
 บ  user-friendly BBS system, and I still don't know half of what PCBoard     บ
 บ  can do because it's so hard to figure out.   I have the 4 commands I      บ
 บ  know and need to use to be able to get around, leech, upload, and read    บ
 บ  messages, and I don't think my knowledge of PCBoard will get much better  บ
 บ  any time soon.   However, you're going to have a hard time arguing that   บ
 บ  any other system is superior.  Why?  Simple.  Try running Renegade in     บ
 บ  multinode.  2 nodes?  Cool.  Try 3.  Still alive?  You're lucky.   Try    บ
 บ  16, like some of the larger boards in the scene (such as Park Central)    บ
 บ  and you'll qickly find a crash.   PCB is the only system I know of that   บ
 บ  can do that so well (except for WildCat, but I don't think I need to      บ
 บ  waste my time commenting).   Still, though, I agree that it would be      บ
 บ  nice if he Renegade modification groups came back around, many single     บ
 บ  node boards still run it.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Krypto                    Interviewee : Dr. Jekyl            บ
 บ    Subject  : Stockade                  Affiliation : n/a                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What exactly is Stockade?                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : Stockade is the mother of all toad blowers.  It's kind of my        บ
 บ        dedication to #Oldwarez.  It's a big old bot, run from my own       บ
 บ        StockServ software, that contains at the time 479 of the best old   บ
 บ        games.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are your current and past affiliations?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : I began with MiRAGE several years back (best run group I've ever    บ
 บ        been in - Thanks Kafka F. Kaska), it then merged and became GRiM.   บ
 บ        GRiM merged with iCE, so I joined a bunch of local groups (CHAOS,   บ
 บ        NARC, MoS), then BoA and after a while iCE.  I quit iCE after 2-3   บ
 บ        days of being in it because I realized that it was all bullshit,    บ
 บ        no sense in being in that kind of group.  I had no affiliations     บ
 บ        for two years until fATE (Fast Action Trade Exchange) stalked me.   บ
 บ        I then joined 8088 which is now a defunct old warez release and     บ
 บ        courier group which fell apart.  I quit fATE and that was it for    บ
 บ        me.  I probably won't join any more groups.  I never got into that  บ
 บ        kr4d 3l33t idea of affiliations anyways.  I can survive on my       บ
 บ        handle alone.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : fATE stalked you, or did a persistent Krypto persuade you to join?  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : Thanks to some friends I made in #Hardwire from the "Under the      บ
 บ        Gate" project on CyberGate, (namely Krypto, Aristotle, and          บ
 บ        Devaste) I hung out in #Fate.  Then, I saw the fATE's diz-tagger,   บ
 บ        and lauged.  I coded a better diz-tagger and Anti Derivative let    บ
 บ        me into the group.  Now my diz-tagger has been all hacked up and    บ
 บ        is used by a lot of courier groups (too bad they never got the      บ
 บ        latest version though).  Then I couriered my sweet will heart out   บ
 บ        (10.5 gigs per day babee!).                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What made you decide to come up with Stockade?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : I started to get interested in old warez back in December when I    บ
 บ        was with fATE.  I began to offer them, and my offer list grew to    บ
 บ        the point of having 131 files on one XDCC List, I plisted in        บ
 บ        #Oldwarez every 45 minutes, until I thought of a better way which   บ
 บ        would be to automatically distribute automated text files with the  บ
 บ        file list/descriptions in them.  Then I worked from there into      บ
 บ        what it is now.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : The newest warez are what people seem to want most and is the       บ
 บ        heart of the business.  Have you seen a similar resurgence in old   บ
 บ        warez?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : Not at all, in fact, I've seen more and more people cramming to     บ
 บ        get into #Oldwarez.  The channel has only grown since I first       บ
 บ        joined it 18 months ago.  People are fed up with 50 disk Doom       บ
 บ        clones that sometimes work, but only on a Pentium 166MHz with 16    บ
 บ        megabytes of RAM.  I think the smart people are the ones dealing    บ
 บ        with #Oldwarez.  Then they're dealing with games that have been     บ
 บ        proven to work, games that are programmed well and games that have  บ
 บ        GAMEPLAY.  I haven't played a game written in the past two years    บ
 บ        with any sense of gameplay in it.  It's all shoot-em-up, bang'em    บ
 บ        out Doom clones and such.  They're all mindless dribble to feed     บ
 บ        the masses I suppose.  What happened to the good stuff such as      บ
 บ        Populous, Curse of the Azure Bonds, King's Quest IV, Dune II,       บ
 บ        etc.?  I feel that the only game released in the past year or so    บ
 บ        with any decent quality is Command and Conquer, but then again, it  บ
 บ        only works well on a Pentium platform.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How much old warez do you pile in every day?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : I get around 40 to 60 megs of uploads per day.  Some of the         บ
 บ        uploaded games are already online, some of the uploaded games       บ
 บ        suck, and some are just way too big or too new.  But there's        บ
 บ        usually about 10-20 games I can pick out per day to add onto the    บ
 บ        bot.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You were originally a member of fATE.  What made you decide to      บ
 บ        leave fATE and was it your plan to leave fATE in order to further   บ
 บ        develop Stockade?                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : Yes, I was originally in fATE (which by the way, was a REAL         บ
 บ        hardcore rocking group, at least when I was in it).  Besides being  บ
 บ        paranoid of my shell administrator, and being fed up with some of   บ
 บ        the really unfair shit going on in groups, I did for a large part   บ
 บ        leave so I could work on the old warez business.  You can say that  บ
 บ        I finally "saw the light" and joined up with the #Oldwarez crew to  บ
 บ        work on Stockade, which was originally nothing more than an         บ
 บ        extremely long XDCC List called "OldJekyl".                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Are you glad you left fATE for the old warez scene?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : I miss a lot of the old fATE crew, but those guys aren't even in    บ
 บ        fATE anymore anyways.  I do miss the 5 am login to the sites,       บ
 บ        writing my DCC lists, and running my XDCC-HTML convertor to make    บ
 บ        the WWW for the slowbies.  There was a sort of a "thrill" involved  บ
 บ        with new warez, an infatuation I suppose.  Everyone wants to try    บ
 บ        the new warez, but in the end, old games are always more sought     บ
 บ        out after.  I'm very glad I left the new shit alone.  The old       บ
 บ        warez scene is more "homely" and down to earth.  And when you get   บ
 บ        a game, you know that there's a 99% chance it's not a fake.  Old    บ
 บ        warez, to put it short and sweet, blows the toad right outta any    บ
 บ        new warez any day of the week.  Well, maybe Windows v1.03 isn't     บ
 บ        that attractive, but I'm referring to games :)                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How often is Stockade accessed every day?                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : Stockade transfers about 500-1000 games a day.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Where do you get most of your files from for Stockade?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : All the warez from Stockade come completely from donations.         บ
 บ        Stockade is Stockade IV right now, which means it's the 4th time    บ
 บ        it's started over from scratch.  In old warez, if you offer, you    บ
 บ        can get mostly any game your heart desires.  So I just called out   บ
 บ        for donations, and then gave those people who donated some leech    บ
 บ        benefits, and so on.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you feel the old warez scene is overlooked and taken for         บ
 บ        granted?                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : Overlooked?  Yes.  It's overlooked by a mass populous of the        บ
 บ        "w4r3z-k1dd13s", which is good.  #Oldwarez isn't a place for        บ
 บ        newbies who don't understand DOS or UNIX.  It's meant for people    บ
 บ        who know what they're doing (for the most part anyways).  I think   บ
 บ        it's advantageous that it's overlooked in that respect.  We         บ
 บ        already have all the good people in it.  I'm not sure how the old   บ
 บ        warez scene can be taken for granted though, every scene is.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Stockade has been down 3 times prior.  What problems can account    บ
 บ        for these 3 shutdowns?                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : I got shut down because of my stupidity.  I used the ISP's          บ
 บ        "ghosted" FTP server as an uploads site.  Once I found out that     บ
 บ        they found the warez, it was instant rm -R.  Stockade II went down  บ
 บ        because of more paranoia.  No biggy.  Stockade III went down        บ
 บ        because I was stupid yet again.  Since my ISP is pretty much        บ
 บ        abandoned, and no one but me really IRCs from it, I decided to      บ
 บ        make the source code world-writable so I could access it from all   บ
 บ        my accounts.  BIG BOOBOO!  One of the ISP dorks, who used to be     บ
 บ        the cosysop of a big warez board in 305 ironically, felt that he    บ
 บ        did not like the fact that I was using up the ISP's resources.  So  บ
 บ        he planted a small backdoor into the code so that whenever I        บ
 บ        updated the .NFO/WWW/.DCC data files, it would email the root, "I   บ
 บ        am the hacker."  The root didn't like that.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Way before you started Stockade, and even before fATE, you were     บ
 บ        involved in a warez operation called "The Gate."  What was that?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : "The Gate" or "Under the Gate" was my experiment in bourne shell    บ
 บ        coding on CyberGate.  I stumbled upon a group of piraters on        บ
 บ        gate.net which had pooled their quota's together so they could get  บ
 บ        warez from each other.  So I then made "The Gate" a BBS-type        บ
 บ        atmosphere (complete with file areas, graffiti walls, etc.), and    บ
 บ        got a few hacked accounts together to create what you could say     บ
 บ        was a 0-day BBS which offered 200 megs of 0-day warez, all run      บ
 บ        from CyberGate.  Unfortunately, one of the system administrators    บ
 บ        noticed that there were lots of users accessing a certain           บ
 บ        directory (even with all my encryption ploys) and managed to bust   บ
 บ        all the hacked accounts along with a few legitimate ones.           บ
 บ        Ironically, I talked to that system administrator a month ago and   บ
 บ        he suggested that I restart CyberGate.  Unfortunatley I'm moving    บ
 บ        to Sweden soon.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Many people had to log onto BBSes to retrieve old warez, was the    บ
 บ        Stockade created as an alternative to this hassle?                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : Stockade was created as a "BBS over IRC" type deal.  Many BBSes do  บ
 บ        not offer old warez anymore.  Stockade is an intelligent tool that  บ
 บ        helps to distribute and increase the variety of old warez in        บ
 บ        #Oldwarez.  I got rather bored of the same old warez being offered  บ
 บ        day in and day out.  I think Stockade has been rather successful.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why is Stockade consisted of only games?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : I used to run a new utils bot as well called [Spatula], but I       บ
 บ        found it was a lot easier to find new utils than old games.  It's   บ
 บ        like looking for today's newspaper, as opposed to trying to find    บ
 บ        the New York times from April, 1947.  I didn't want to offer old    บ
 บ        utils, because they're useless.  I find it more of a joke than      บ
 บ        anything else.  I deleted [Spatula] eventually because I wanted to  บ
 บ        have the hard disk space to further expand the library of games     บ
 บ        found on Stockade.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I've noticed the offer bot's online handle changes ever so          บ
 บ        frequently.  Why is this done?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : The handle changes quite frequently due to the evils of word of     บ
 บ        mouth.  While I do like the fact that many people are using         บ
 บ        Stockade, I don't want many of the WRONG people using Stockade.     บ
 บ        This prevents people from channels other than #Oldwarez from using  บ
 บ        Stockade, and so mean old nasty NARC's don't find it...             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is Stockade run off a custom sript or is it based on other          บ
 บ        offering scripts?                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : The "HEART" of Stockade is StockServ v2.1, which is my own 100%     บ
 บ        original design, coded in 100% bourne shell (bourne shell is 100%   บ
 บ        compatible on EVERY ISP) which automatically creates the DCC        บ
 บ        datafile, NFO file, and the optional WWW.  StockServ interacts      บ
 บ        with IRC via a frontend, which is your standard every day IRC       บ
 บ        script tweaked to support StockServ.  It comes in two flavors       บ
 บ        right now, VeNoM and Atlantis, and eventually there will be Fluff   บ
 บ        Phoenix and mIRC (via a DOS version of StockServ due out soon).     บ
 บ        The brilliant part of StockServ is that there's NO compiling        บ
 บ        required (for those hard-assed administrators who don't allow it),  บ
 บ        and that you can actually IRC your bot as if it were a normal IRC   บ
 บ        script.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : All files on Stockade are free, correct?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : Stockade is 100% free with no minimum transfer speeds.  I would     บ
 บ        never operate any differently.  The only restriction is the number  บ
 บ        of slots, which is 3 for non-donators, and unlimited for donators.  บ
 บ        #Oldwarez is about free unrestricted old warez.  Therefore, so is   บ
 บ        Stockade.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Stockade was once available via the WWW.  What happened to this     บ
 บ        option?                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : StockServ does automatically program the WWW interface, but the     บ
 บ        reason why Stockade no longer has a WWW site is that there are no   บ
 บ        longer any fast anonymous FTP's for me to use.  So alas, it's only  บ
 บ        IRC this time.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Where can people go for more information on Stockade?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : To begin with, don't bother the people in #Oldwarez about it.       บ
 บ        They get annoyed about it and they won't crack either.  You can     บ
 บ        message me, I'll probably be away though, if I like you, I might    บ
 บ        reply.  But the best way to get on Stockade would be to get         บ
 บ        involved with #Oldwarez, just hang out with the crew.  Lamers need  บ
 บ        not bother.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Where should people send their donations?                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DRJ : Just DCC them over to me.  If they're old, and not too insanely     บ
 บ        huge, I'll add it to the Stockade.  By the way, a Stockade CD is    บ
 บ        in the works.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Krypto                    Interviewee : Desys                บ
 บ    Subject  : Motiv8                    Affiliation : Motiv8 Council       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is your current position in Motiv8?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : I am Motiv8 Council.  I basically watch over the group, find fast   บ
 บ        couriers, and fast FTP sites, etc.  I also protect the channel.  I  บ
 บ        make sure the group doesn't die like the rumors say it's going to   บ
 บ        happen.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How was M8 founded?                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : Well, I am not fimilar with all the history.  I know that MASON     บ
 บ        founded it.  He's still with us.  It had some people that left and  บ
 บ        quit.  Igor was a council member along with Davan when I merged     บ
 บ        tNt with M8 but they quit within a week.  So I had to take the      บ
 บ        place of Davan/Igor by watching the group and Davan's job           บ
 บ        "couriering".  I do a little couriering to some of our FTP sites.   บ
 บ        I also do what Igor was supposed to do which was to watch the       บ
 บ        group make sure it never dies, etc.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : In recent news, Davan and Igor left M8.  How can you account for    บ
 บ        him leaving?                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : Well I think they both left for perfectly good reasons.  Davan      บ
 บ        didn't almost kill the group the night he left.  Igor almost did    บ
 บ        though because obviously he did most of the work for months, which  บ
 บ        shouldn't happen in a group.  It's very hard running a 1 man group  บ
 บ        and some couriers.  Igor always loved M8 but MASON just wasn't      บ
 บ        showing up so Igor quit for MALiCE and Davan quit for Amnesia,      บ
 บ        both of which are top groups and I don't blame them.  I just        บ
 บ        wished they'd give it another week.  Oh well, but like I said,      บ
 บ        Igor left for a reason and I agree with his actions.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How has Igor's absence effected M8?                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : Well Igor had a FTP site that he was co-site operator on.  One of   บ
 บ        the best in the world.  We lost it when he went to MALiCE.  He      บ
 บ        made sure everyone was cool and just hearing the fact that Igor     บ
 บ        left made couple top people quit for other groups.  Oh well, I've   บ
 บ        got the group doing a lot better.  I got FTP sites and couriers.    บ
 บ        Unlike other groups I have a real easy time finding FTP sites.  I   บ
 บ        find us 2 a week usually, we currently got quite a few.  That's     บ
 บ        what's keeping us alive, our FTP sites and site operators.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : For what reasons do you feel Davan left M8?                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : Davan quit for the same reason.  Davan was just a courier in most   บ
 บ        people's opinions.  He did good, but he made the couriering part    บ
 บ        for us great along with Igor.  Davan was offered to go to Amnesia   บ
 บ        and they are mostly winning everywhere along with RiSC, DGT,        บ
 บ        MALiCE, RTS, or whatever you think.  When he left, it didn't        บ
 บ        really hurt us but his couriering hurt us.  When Igor quit, THAT    บ
 บ        almost killed us.  Most of the members knew that Igor ran the       บ
 บ        group for the most part.  He merged M8 with tNt so M8 wouldn't die  บ
 บ        after he left.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Approximately how many people have left M8 since the tNt merger?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : About 5 people have left, but these people were like Davan, Igor,   บ
 บ        Caserd, and a couple others.  That is ok, I thought it'd be a lot   บ
 บ        more but I've replaced them all besides Igor, cause you can't       บ
 บ        replace him.  He basically kept the group alive then.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Could you explain to us why there was a merger between M8 and tNt   บ
 บ        to begin with?                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : Well tnt noticed M8 offered quite a few FTP sites which tNt was     บ
 บ        losing on through the summer.  I wanted a lot more top couriers,    บ
 บ        also we had 2 or 3 GREAT couriers.  Now we have a lot of people     บ
 บ        that are capable and I am accepting people who can courier like a   บ
 บ        gig if that much is released each week.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What effect has the merger brought about?                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : Well, we're twice as powerful with M8 and we are doing better with  บ
 บ        all these FTP sites.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : No regrets in merging with tNt?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : None.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : It's well known of M8's strength in FTP sites.  Considering most    บ
 บ        FTP sites are college based, many of them will go down this         บ
 บ        summer.  How do you feel this will effect M8?                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : Actually, I have managed to find us TONS of FTP sites that are up   บ
 บ        in the summer, which most groups can't do.  Well that's a strength  บ
 บ        and I blocked the hole that made us lose all these FTP sites.       บ
 บ        Yes, we have lost a few but oh well...                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Aside from the SMALL breakup in M8, what other problems has M8      บ
 บ        faced in the past?                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : Well, just these rumors and other couriering groups stealing our    บ
 บ        FTP sites and couriers.  I have tried to get them back and that's   บ
 บ        about it.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Since the #Fatefiles days, #M8Leech was not rather successful.      บ
 บ        But in recent days, #M8Leech is now comparable to today's #Exceed   บ
 บ        (#Exceed was previously known as #Fatefiles).  How do you account   บ
 บ        for this recent success?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : Well basically, I ignore #M8Leech for reasons most people do.  FTP  บ
 บ        sites are fine with me.  I'll let the IRC division run that which   บ
 บ        I usually don't touch.  Another problem is that we have to find     บ
 บ        bots and people to get the channel back which is a big hassle.      บ
 บ        #Exceed is loaded with people you never want to meet, if you catch  บ
 บ        my drift.  #M8Leech is turning just as bad.  So I tell the IRC      บ
 บ        division to just have fun since I really don't care :)              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Which groups does M8 courier for?                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : We recently lost SODOM.. BIG DEAL.  We gained SiVA and we're still  บ
 บ        couriering for UCF.  But all around we'll courier for anyone at a   บ
 บ        moment's notice.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are M8's current goals and plans for the future?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : We're trying to make a strong FTP trading team by getting LOADS of  บ
 บ        FTP sites with our couriers.  I also want M8 to be one of top 5     บ
 บ        courier groups in most people's opinion and to let me senior a      บ
 บ        little less and courier a little more.  If I can work on            บ
 บ        organization and get more FTP sites, that'll make it all fun.       บ
 บ        Also, I just want us to HAVE FUN.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : In all honesty, should you have to rank M8 amongst the other        บ
 บ        courier groups, where would you place yourselves?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : Well, M8's about fifth or sixth.  RiSC is #1, DGT and AMN is #2     บ
 บ        and #3, RTS is #4, and we're about equal with Empire.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Which do you feel is stronger, your Internet division or BBS        บ
 บ        spreading division?                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : That's the easy question.  INTERNET!!!  BBSes are getting too old   บ
 บ        and outdated.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What do you feel are M8's strengths?                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : M8's best at FTP and IRC couriering.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What do you feel are M8's weaknesses?                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : Uhhh... we have to get more organized.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you in any way feel M8 hasn't been getting the respect it        บ
 บ        deserves or is underrated?                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : Yes, I don't think people should get greedy and steal FTP sites     บ
 บ        and couriers, but that's life.  These little lamers in some group   บ
 บ        last week said they could beat the whole M8 team with their 2400    บ
 บ        baud modems which.. NO NAMES...                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What are some prospects you feel about the scene?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  DES : Well the scene's summer is gonna be lagged a bit due to FTP sites   บ
 บ        down people, me getting a life, etc.  Unless you want kill your     บ
 บ        summer, the scene's summer will be slow.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Sailor Moon          บ
 บ    Subject  : Moon Prism.. Power!!!     Affiliation : Sailor Moon          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What kind of group is Sailor Moon and how did it start up?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : Well, we're five models from Miami, Florida.  We all work in the    บ
 บ        same modeling studio and so we decided to rent an apartment         บ
 บ        between the five of us.  The studio sent us a computer along with   บ
 บ        some Internet software to work with, I don't know why they sent us  บ
 บ        one, we're models, we don't really have a need for computers.  All  บ
 บ        we have to do is look good in front of the camera.  Anyways,        บ
 บ        Sailor Venus started messing around on IRC and we stumbled upon     บ
 บ        warez.  Sailor Venus' boytoy (men are just toys meant for           บ
 บ        beautiful women to abuse) is a district manager of Egghead.  So     บ
 บ        Sailor Venus started teaching him about the Internet, and soon,     บ
 บ        got us all hooked on it.  We realized that Sailor Venus' boytoy     บ
 บ        could help us supply with some new warez, we decided to help out    บ
 บ        the scene, and thus, we formed Sailor Moon.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why did you name your group after yourself?                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : I didn't.  We're all big fans of the Japanese Animation "Sailor     บ
 บ        Moon : Pretty Soldier" (the North American version translated by    บ
 บ        DIC is horrible compared to the original Japanese series).          บ
 บ        Anyways, we realized that we wanted to name our group after         บ
 บ        something we liked, and I came up with the idea to start the        บ
 บ        group, so I named myself Sailor Moon, and gave my 4 roommates       บ
 บ        handles as well.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I've been seeing a lot of warez released lately by your group,      บ
 บ        Sailor Moon, some of them were useless PUD files (aka WarCraft II   บ
 บ        Expansion Set : Beyond the Dark Portal), and the rest were          บ
 บ        basically kids software.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : We really don't care about that quality and quantity bullshit.      บ
 บ        When Sailor Venus' boyfriend gets us a release, we attach the       บ
 บ        diz/nfo and we send it via our T1.  We don't have time to worry     บ
 บ        about any other bullshit.  If you were living with us, you'd        บ
 บ        understand what being a model is like; we have hectic schedules     บ
 บ        everyday and we can only find time for releasing on weekends.  You  บ
 บ        can look at us as a very relaxed group, we don't even have a        บ
 บ        public IRC channel.  We all live together, if we want something     บ
 บ        done, I just talk to my friends.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You only have one supplier I assume?  Do you feel that is enough    บ
 บ        to sustain your group?  What is the handle of your supplier?        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : We haven't given him a handle yet, and we aren't planning to.  You  บ
 บ        see, Sailor Moon is a girls group only.  We're not looking for any  บ
 บ        more suppliers, and we're not looking for any more members.  If we  บ
 บ        like someone and we think they can help the group, I'll just        บ
 บ        approach them face to face.  Our modeling studio is my recruiting   บ
 บ        ground.  If you're not a model, don't even bother applying.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How old are the members of Sailor Moon?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : I'm 23, Sailor Mercury is 22, Sailor Venus is 21, Sailor Mars is    บ
 บ        23, and Sailor Jupiter is 22.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Since you didn't mention Sailor Venus' boyfriend as a member, I     บ
 บ        assume he isn't one?                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : You're correct, we don't consider him a member, he's just a friend  บ
 บ        of ours.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How have you spread your warez in the past?  You have not accepted  บ
 บ        any courier applications I assume, or any applications at all?      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : We have covert contacts with couriers from RiSC, Amnesia, and       บ
 บ        fATE.  We just dcc it to them and they take care of the spreading   บ
 บ        for us.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is Sailor Moon planning on having official couriers?                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : That bullshit?  Yeah.. sure.. we don't even have time to mess with  บ
 บ        an IRC channel and you think we'll want to have official couriers?  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Argh.. sorry for asking.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  SMO : It's ok.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ      I talked to her on the phone later that day, but could not convince   บ
 บ  her to tell me which magazines she's been in, or to send me one of her    บ
 บ  photo shoots in gif or jpg format.  She sounded like a really nice        บ
 บ  person over the phone, but she sounded awfully bitchy over IRC (kind      บ
 บ  of reminds me of Winterhawk, but Winterhawk is not exactly a model).      บ
 บ  She's a model, I guess it's natural for her to act that way.              บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Marbz                บ
 บ    Subject  : Empire                    Affiliation : Empire President     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : A few months ago, you were the President of a jumpstart courier     บ
 บ        group called dCS (Designated Courier Specialists).  It didnt'       บ
 บ        surprise me much that it died within a week.  It lacked             บ
 บ        leadership, talent, and enthusiasm, along with many other things    บ
 บ        found in a good courier group.  However, right after dCS died, I    บ
 บ        saw that you immediately became the President of another new        บ
 บ        courier group, Empire.  Empire has not only outlived the one week   บ
 บ        group stage, but it's survived for months now and is showing its    บ
 บ        presence in the scene.  How'd you do it Marbz?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MAR : dCS was more of a learning experience for me and for most of my     บ
 บ        members, from that experience I met some good traders and got more  บ
 บ        insight on how to run shit.  Then I decided to do it right this     บ
 บ        second time with Empire and now here I am.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So one day, you were running dCS, and then you said to yourself,    บ
 บ        "I'm not doing this right", and the very next day, you came up      บ
 บ        with.. Empire?  That's how your groups evolved?  It must have been  บ
 บ        more than a one day thing.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MAR : Haha.. no it took me a few weeks to realize dCS was going           บ
 บ        downhill.  I just thought some things over and tried to work some   บ
 บ        shit out.  But when it came down to it, I really didnt have the     บ
 บ        members nor the leadership I needed to keep it together.  So I      บ
 บ        talked to some of the guys I thought were doing a good job and who  บ
 บ        knew what they were doing, and we decided to form Empire.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So not everyone from dCS made it to Empire, you had to do some      บ
 บ        "CUTTING" hey?  You felt that dCS was going downhill and that you   บ
 บ        didn't have the leadership?  So you LACKED leadership qualities     บ
 บ        while you were the President of dCS, how then, did you suddenly     บ
 บ        develop your skills, or did you start Empire with a friend, and he  บ
 บ        provided the needed leadership, and thus, deserves the real credit  บ
 บ        for making Empire what it is today, a very strong upcoming courier  บ
 บ        group.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MAR : Not everyone from dCS made it to Empire.  In fact only a few did.   บ
 บ        The mistake I made with dCS was that I was too easy in letting      บ
 บ        members in.  I didn't check up on them.  I didn't even put them on  บ
 บ        trial.  The other major thing that didn't happen was my seniors.    บ
 บ        They were just plain lazy and never helped out.  So I just started  บ
 บ        talking to some other leaders and shit and picked up pointers here  บ
 บ        and there.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Yes, I can tell you've improved a lot just by looking at your       บ
 บ        Empire NFO, I can see some very big names.  Our readers, some of    บ
 บ        who will some day run their own groups, would like to know, how     บ
 บ        you recruited such big names.  For example, how'd you recruit       บ
 บ        "Arch Magi", who runs a 13 node ISDN board (ex-Razor 1911 Courier   บ
 บ        HQ, ex-Legacy World HQ). Also, how'd you recruit "Mike and Dave"    บ
 บ        one of the BEST long distance bluebox couriers from Holland?        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MAR : Well, mainly just by being in the scene and meeting new people.     บ
 บ        That's all you can really do in order to start getting familiar     บ
 บ        with the scene and how it works.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How would you rate Empire compared to the big groups such as RiSC,  บ
 บ        Amnesia, Digital, and fATE?  A lot of people are starting to        บ
 บ        consider Empire one of the top courier groups?  How has Empire      บ
 บ        been successful in the scene compared to the other groups?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MAR : I don't feel that Empire is ready to compete to its full            บ
 บ        potential.  RiSC has been in the scene for some time and their      บ
 บ        leaders know what they are doing and have the experience.  Empire   บ
 บ        isn't mature enought YET.  They've been around the block and they   บ
 บ        know what they are doing.  I don't really know a lot about Amnesia  บ
 บ        but they look to me like they know what the fuck they are doing.    บ
 บ        In this point in time I don't feel that Empire has the experience   บ
 บ        to compete against them but in the long run, we'll make it up to    บ
 บ        their status.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Well, at least you're being honest, but you forgot to mention       บ
 บ        about fATE and Digital?                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MAR : I'd rather not please.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How many private FTP sites do Empire members have access to?        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MAR : We currently have 4 private FTP sites.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Many courier groups have sites which are run through connections    บ
 บ        through their college.  And thus, many courier groups take a big    บ
 บ        hit when summer time rolls along and all the college linked sites   บ
 บ        go down, will summer time have a big effect for Empire?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MAR : Yes, Empire will be losing 2 sites because of it and those 2 sites  บ
 บ        are run by some of our best members.  Yes, it will definitely       บ
 บ        effect us.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is Empire official couriers for any release groups?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MAR : We have had oppurtunites to become official for some very large     บ
 บ        groups but have not taken up on the offer.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Which groups?                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MAR : I cannot say.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why did you not take up their offers?                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MAR : Well, for one thing they weren't very organised.  They could        บ
 บ        release, but I could tell that they were not as active as they      บ
 บ        were a few years back.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Since Empire is not officials for anyone, do you find it hard to    บ
 บ        find stuff to tag?  Do you guys tag at all, double tag, or strip    บ
 บ        tag?                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MAR : We will NEVER double or strip tag because theres no point in doing  บ
 บ        that.  But yes, we do tag if we find a new warez that's not been    บ
 บ        tagged.  Since most of our traders are in other release groups we   บ
 บ        can get a release the minute it's released.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you courier warez that's been tagged by Empire? or do you guys   บ
 บ        still courier anything and everything regardless of who tagged it?  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  MAR : Yes, we trade all warez.  If they are tagged we don't tag them.     บ
 บ        We just kindly pass the warez along.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : The Wicked One       บ
 บ    Subject  : MindCrash???  Uh...       Affiliation : DMT President        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : A few months ago, you were once the president of top-notch courier  บ
 บ        group known as MC (MindCrash).  However, it died mysteriously and   บ
 บ        many are not aware of your new ventures.  But before we get to      บ
 บ        your new group, let's go through how MC died?                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TWO : MC got to be so big and out of hand that trouble was erupting       บ
 บ        everywhere.  I had to leave the scene for a period due to having    บ
 บ        to get other things straightened out.  When I left, I put Avoozl    บ
 บ        in charge (Avoozl had left the group before due to outside          บ
 บ        problems).  Many people thought my vice-president, Blitzkrieg       บ
 บ        should have been put in charge, and the only reason I did not       บ
 บ        leave him in charge was that I could talk to Avoozl voice every     บ
 บ        day and in that way, still semi-run the group.  People started      บ
 บ        saying that maybe Blitzkrieg should start his own group, which he   บ
 บ        did, called IMP (Impulse).                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Did you know beforehand that Blitzkrieg was planning to start his   บ
 บ        own courier group?                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TWO : Yes.  Knowing beforehand what was going to happen, Avoozl and I     บ
 บ        decided to just abandon the MC name altogether and start fresh      บ
 บ        with something new.  Blitzkrieg's group quickly merged into DGT     บ
 บ        (Digital).  We took the main ideal of quality and offered MC's      บ
 บ        best couriers a spot in the new group.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is the name of your new group?                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TWO : We call ourselves DMT (DarkMoon Traders).                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How many members are there in DMT?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TWO : DMT is currently consisted of about 20 members.  Of the 20          บ
 บ        members, 7 are site operators.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When your new group started up, did you invite all your old MC      บ
 บ        members, or only some?  If you invited only some, did you invite    บ
 บ        Blitzkrieg and Devast into DMT?  Blitzkrieg and Devast are          บ
 บ        currently DGT leaders, who were both ex-MC.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TWO : I only invited the top members of MC.  Only 3 of the people who     บ
 บ        were invited did not come with me.  I did not invite Blitzkrieg     บ
 บ        because he was heavy into making his new group.  Devast was kicked  บ
 บ        out of MC a long time ago and he has never forgotten it, so I did   บ
 บ        not think it would be a good idea to make him a part of DMT.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Who were the 3 people who rejected your proposal?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TWO : The 3 people who rejected my proposal were, Swamper who is now in   บ
 บ        Digital, Tutt who is now in.. I have no clue, and Chrome who is     บ
 บ        now in Motiv8.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You mentioned to me earlier that your group works underground, why  บ
 บ        have you kept DMT's presence underground?  Will it not make it      บ
 บ        harder for good couriers and site operators to apply for the        บ
 บ        group?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TWO : Yes, it is very hard to get in touch with DMT.  If they're good     บ
 บ        enough, they'll find us.  The reason we decided to keep it          บ
 บ        underground is that it keeps our members hidden from federal        บ
 บ        agents.  It gives an added element of security.  Besides, we        บ
 บ        aren't into egos and we're all past that bullshit.  We don't need   บ
 บ        people to TELL us we're good, we KNOW we're good.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : So you guys don't even have an NFO?                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TWO : Our NFO file only has an email address where you can reach us, and  บ
 บ        a little information about the group at the bottom.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Since DMT is so underground, how would someone apply?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TWO : To get in touch with DMT, just email changj@webe.hooked.net.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : If you look at DMT in it's current status, do you think it's        บ
 บ        reached the level MC reached during its peak a few months back?     บ
 บ        Do you believe you'll be able to repeat the magic twice?            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TWO : DMT lacks the numbers of MC, but the quality of the couriers is     บ
 บ        much better overall.  There is no question as to what everyone's    บ
 บ        purpose is in the group, and with time DMT will easily become       บ
 บ        better than MC ever was.  I don't know if I can repeat magic, but   บ
 บ        I'm still the same person, I just work a little more efficiently,   บ
 บ        and have more top-notch couriers to work with.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Even though DMT is underground, have you guys attempted to recruit  บ
 บ        official release groups to courier for?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TWO : We attempted to recruit Fierce at one time, but Fierce chose DGT.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Have you encountered any problems with old MC members while         บ
 บ        starting DMT?                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TWO : There have hardly been any problems at all.  It's been an easy      บ
 บ        transition, our members are so dedicated I must give all credit to  บ
 บ        them.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : There are groups such as Everlast that have gone underground and    บ
 บ        many consider that they're at least as good as RiSC if not better,  บ
 บ        which only goes to show that an underground group is by far NOT     บ
 บ        handicapped because it is underground.  Do you feel that DMT will   บ
 บ        be considered in competition in the same manner as Everlast is to   บ
 บ        the rest of the scene?                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TWO : Everlast is made up of guys who stick together and are a team much  บ
 บ        like DMT.  They let the work they do speak for themselves, as do    บ
 บ        we.                                                                 บ

 บ    Subject  : PTA Beeeaaaach!!!         Affiliation : PTA President        บ

 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
