 บ  RCN : PTA (Power Trading Arsenal) Couriers have been around for a few     บ
 บ        weeks now, and has started to show its presence in the couriering   บ
 บ        scene, where did it spawn from?  Why did you decide to create PTA?  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  IMP : I started by joining DiC (Domination In Couriering).  I became a    บ
 บ        small BBS Courier for them.  Then Blackened (President of DiC)      บ
 บ        killed DiC and joined fATE, I was left with no group to courier     บ
 บ        for.  I then heard that one of the vice-presidents of DiC was in    บ
 บ        the process of creating a new courier group called FCC (First       บ
 บ        Class Couriering).  I became the art coordinator for FCC and soon   บ
 บ        became FCC's general coordinator.  FCC then changed its name to     บ
 บ        SMC (Smooth Moving Couriers).  One day, the President of FCC told   บ
 บ        me that he no longer had the time to run the group, so I took over  บ
 บ        the group, and within a week, I changed its name to PTA since SMC   บ
 บ        was already in use.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : There are already tons of couriering groups out there, what makes   บ
 บ        PTA different?  How wil it stand out from the rest?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  IMP : We will stand out from the rest because all our couriers are        บ
 บ        dedicated.  We have worked EXTREMELY hard to get to where we are    บ
 บ        at.  We don't double or strip tag, and our group is made up of a    บ
 บ        circle of friends.  We have come to trust one another.  We are all  บ
 บ        dedicated to our job immensely.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Through that trust, have you encountred any problems running the    บ
 บ        group or in getting people to improve in their couriering           บ
 บ        abilities?  What happens when someone slacks off and gets lazy?     บ
 บ        Will you kick a FRIEND out of your group, or is he allowed to take  บ
 บ        leave when needed?                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  IMP : Well, if a member gets lazy, which a few have, we will give them    บ
 บ        time to make a comeback.  If they don't put in any effort, I will   บ
 บ        personally talk with the member, find out the problems and we will  บ
 บ        make an agreement.  Either they agree to go down a position or      บ
 บ        work harder.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : That is a very good method.  How many members are there in PTA?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  IMP : We have approximately 35 members.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : How many Private FTP sites are run by PTA?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  IMP : We currently have access to 2 private FTP sites.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Many courier groups enter a slump during the summer because         บ
 บ        they're site operators who have to leave their college during the   บ
 บ        summer break, will that have an effect on any of PTA's sites?       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  IMP : It may have an effect on 1 site, but we will most likely have a     บ
 บ        new one soon so we will always have the same ammount of stable      บ
 บ        sites until school is back, then we will have all 3 together once   บ
 บ        more.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : You are a very new leader since you have not had anyone to learn    บ
 บ        leadership skills from.  You were in a group called DiC which died  บ
 บ        in a matter of weeks, do you feel that PTA might turn out to be a   บ
 บ        group with no potential as the weeks roll by?  What are your        บ
 บ        future plans for PTA?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  IMP : I've always been a good leader.  I run a really successfull art     บ
 บ        group that does work for 613/819 area.  We are the dominating       บ
 บ        artists of that area.  I feel that we have a lot of potential.  I   บ
 บ        try not to make any bad mistakes, and I haven't made any bad        บ
 บ        mistakes so far.  I think before I act, and I'm a nice guy.  I      บ
 บ        don't get pissed off at people for nothing.  I am friends with a    บ
 บ        lot of presidents around the scene.  My plans for PTA is to become  บ
 บ        feared by other courier groups.  I want PTA to become widely        บ
 บ        known.  I want newbies to look up to PTA like how many look up to   บ
 บ        RiSC and fATE.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Great, so your main goal in the scene is to become well known, do   บ
 บ        you feel that as your group does gain it's deserved respect, that   บ
 บ        your group trust might fall apart since members might be striving   บ
 บ        toward selfishness and ego trips?                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  IMP : I don't think many other courier groups respect us yet.  The trust  บ
 บ        won't fall apart because were all friends.  Anyone that's gets off  บ
 บ        on an ego trip will be approached, and given a little reality       บ
 บ        check (no pun intended).  If they don't realize what they're        บ
 บ        doing, then the other seniors and I talk it over with them.  I      บ
 บ        work with each and every member personally, some presidents I know  บ
 บ        don't even know half his members.  I want total control over my     บ
 บ        group.  I want to keep it on track.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Is there a central message that you'd like to inform the scene      บ
 บ        concerning PTA?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  IMP : I'd like to say that PTA is not a group of '3L1T3 Pricks'.  I'd     บ
 บ        also like to thank Locutous.  He's been one of the best members     บ
 บ        I've ever worked with.  He's helped the group a lot and is greatly  บ
 บ        appreciated.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Super Hacker              Interviewee : Incarnate            บ
 บ    Subject  : RCN/Road Rebel            Affiliation : Ex-ROR Senior        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is your opinion of RCN as an E-Zine group?                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  INC : Well, I think it has done well in the past.  But, it's reputation   บ
 บ        was basically ruined because of the incident.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : "The Incident"?  Can you explain what you mean by the incident?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  INC : To make a long story short.  Wave Rider had a disagreement with     บ
 บ        Road Rebel over the supply of a certain program to Legacy           บ
 บ        Entertainment, and RoadRebel called up a beta tester for that       บ
 บ        company and "Narqed" on WaveRider, and well, The rest is history.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you feel RCN has potential as an E-Zine group?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  INC : Not now, RCN will only have potential if it drops Road Rebel        บ
 บ        immediately and in turn recruits someone more productive such as    บ
 บ        Entropy.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you have anything personal against Road Rebel?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  INC : Yes, I do.  Wave Rider is a friend of mine and he suffered just     บ
 บ        because Road Rebel wanted to be an ASSHOLE, he took it WAY TOO      บ
 บ        FAR.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What trouble did Wave Rider get into?                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  INC : No comment.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Would you read RCN magazine even though Road Rebel is still in the  บ
 บ        group?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  INC : No, I would not.  And I'm going to spread the word as far as        บ
 บ        possible to tell people not to spread it on any boards or on any    บ
 บ        FTP sites.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : If Road Rebel wasn't a part of RCN, would you be a regular reader   บ
 บ        of RCN?                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  INC : Probably.  People such as Road Rebel should be dragged out into     บ
 บ        the street and shot.  This damn box in front of me is supposed to   บ
 บ        used for FUN.  It wasn't made so some asshole could get you in      บ
 บ        deep trouble.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Incarnate,                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Not only are you not aware of the whole story of which you so         บ
 บ  self-righteously call "The Incident", you also take it upon yourself to   บ
 บ  rack on a very special friend of mine, ROAD REBEL.  Neither I nor Hitex   บ
 บ  would give a care in the world whether or not Road Rebel's membership     บ
 บ  does effect RCN's reputation.  Road Rebel is a part of RCN, and he's      บ
 บ  staying a part of RCN, whether you like it or not...                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                              - Rebel Chicken [RCN Editor]  บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Super Hacker              Interviewee : Univers              บ
 บ    Subject  : ME Scared??  FOOEY!!!     Affiliation : n/a                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Who are you and how long have you being in the scene?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UNI : I was the President of AOF (Arsenists on Fire).  I was also a       บ
 บ        member of DMN (Demolition), ROR (Release on Rampage), and MTY       บ
 บ        (Mortality).  I've been in the scene for about 2 years now but I    บ
 บ        was kicked in November of 1995.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : I see you were the President of a group that actually lasted        บ
 บ        longer than 2 months, a group that actually released a few worth    บ
 บ        while games and utils.  Why did you leave AOF?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UNI : I didn't actually want to leave AOF, I was "forced" to resign.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Why were you forced to resign and by whom?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UNI : Well, I was forced to leave because Tha Stuff, Demon, and           บ
 บ        Skyscraper said that I was an immature President and that I can't   บ
 บ        run a group.  AOF was a releasing group, we released a few          บ
 บ        releases and a release that DOD duped.  We had a lot of really      บ
 บ        talented suppliers, a few from Borland and Microsoft.  Skyscraper   บ
 บ        said that I could stay and supply for them, but I thought about     บ
 บ        it, from being a President to being a supplier, it was not a good   บ
 บ        deal.  A month after my forced resignation, I saw that it had       บ
 บ        merged into COPS, BLAH!                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What is your current opinion on COPS?  There are serveral members   บ
 บ        stating that "COPS is lame and they have to get their shit          บ
 บ        together."                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UNI : I think that COPS can be "okay" if they put their shit together,    บ
 บ        like you said, and I don't think that they are very organized,      บ
 บ        especially not if they release shit like BLAKE STONE, a program     บ
 บ        from 1993 with an engine similar to Wolfenstine 3D.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : When you were forced to resign as President of AOF, did you just    บ
 บ        leave?  After all, you were the President, you should have at       บ
 บ        least had some power in the way things got done.  Was there a lack  บ
 บ        of leadership from your part, or were there power struggles         บ
 บ        between seniors and members, or was there just a lot of the same    บ
 บ        old ego bullshit?                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UNI : Well, I didn't feel like having a fight with Tha Stuff, I thought   บ
 บ        he deserved a little bit more power, so I made him vice-president,  บ
 บ        I think he got a little carried away with "power".                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Do you regret leaving AOF?                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UNI : I don't regret leaving AOF, I think that I learned a lot from       บ
 บ        leaving.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : What groups are you currently affiliated with?                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UNI : I am not affiliated as of yet.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : "As of yet"?  I see that you are getting back into the scene soon   บ
 บ        then?  What are your future plans?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UNI : I think I might try to join a highly respected releasing group, or  บ
 บ        maybe getting a FTP site and then joining PWA or DOD.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  RCN : Are you comfortable coming back into the scene?  Do you feel that   บ
 บ        Tha Stuff, Demon, or Skyscraper might bug you or harass you in any  บ
 บ        way?                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  UNI : Hehehe, I ain't scared SHIT of Tha Stuff, Demon, Skyscraper, or     บ
 บ        anyone else.  Just one little extra comment, Revolution-X should    บ
 บ        merge into COPS, that way, both groups can be lame together.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Subject : Drapper *BUSTED*                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      On Sunday, May 19th, RCN issue #14 was released on channel #RCN at    บ
 บ  approximately 9 pm Eastern Standard Time.  Included in every issue of     บ
 บ  RCN is a Warez-IQ test, and on this particular test, there included a     บ
 บ  question as follows :                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ๐5๐ Drapper runs a FTP site from this well known college/university :     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      [ ] A. University of California Berkeley                              บ
 บ      [ ] B. Diablo Valley College                                          บ
 บ      [ ] C. Harvard and Radcliffe Colleges                                 บ
 บ      [๛] D. Massachusetts Institute of Technology                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The correct answer to the above question is "D".  Drapper informed    บ
 บ  RCN at 1:30 am of the next day that his FTP site called "The Temple"      บ
 บ  was *BUSTED* by MIT personnel as a result of RCN's quiz question.  In     บ
 บ  theory, if what Drapper said was true, then it is safe to say that        บ
 บ  within a timespan of 4 hours, the MIT personnel downloaded RCN issue      บ
 บ  #14, read the Warez-IQ Questions, and in shock, got a warrant to *BUST*   บ
 บ  Drapper's FTP site.  It is also safe to assume that if Drapper's story    บ
 บ  was true, then the MIT personnel considers the information found in RCN   บ
 บ  to be quite accurate, and accurate enough that they would bust someone    บ
 บ  without consulting other possible references.  Not only that, the MIT     บ
 บ  personnel would have to had bust Drapper sometime between 9pm and 1:30am  บ
 บ  on a Sunday night.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In reality, none of what Drapper said occurred.  He was not busted,   บ
 บ  and if his FTP site, "The Temple", was not operative during the week,     บ
 บ  it's only because he took it down of his onw accord in a pathetic         บ
 บ  attempt of winning people's sympathy.  Fortunately, people are smart      บ
 บ  enough not to believe in his recently concocted story.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Defender Zeta                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Pirate Boot Camp                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This article is for all the newbie traders out there who would like   บ
 บ  to jump to the next level in the scene but don't know what to do once     บ
 บ  they get into a group.  Thise article was written to help beginners       บ
 บ  learn some of the tricks that more experienced couriers know.  Most       บ
 บ  traders learn this stuff from trial and error <mostly error> or with the  บ
 บ  help of an older trader who acts as a tutor.  I have to take the time     บ
 บ  now to thank Ratz Blood and Ratphour for teaching me the ins and outs of  บ
 บ  the scene.  I would still be a #Fatefiles whore if it were not for them.  บ
 บ  Let's begin :)                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  BBS (Bulletin Board Service)                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Way back when the scene was not on the Internet, couriers were the    บ
 บ  people who couriered warez from a HQ BBS to the distro sites.  Some       บ
 บ  phreaked the long distance, others carded the long distance.  I don't     บ
 บ  encourage carding since it is not only dangerous, but it could easily     บ
 บ  get a newbie busted.  Phreaking is no longer used.  The best strategy     บ
 บ  for a courier who wishes to mark his or her place in the scene would be   บ
 บ  to get a local distro site for some courier group to sponsor you into     บ
 บ  the group.  Have the system operator bitch out a senior until he gives    บ
 บ  you a chance.  Get access to the leech sites and start and downloading    บ
 บ  and and uploading.  It's pretty simple.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      BBS couriers on big BBSes where the competition is stiff usually get  บ
 บ  a big hard drive quota on their shell account.  Don't PPP download, FTP   บ
 บ  site operators hate it, plus there's always the problem of having the     บ
 บ  FTP site going down for a few minutes right before your transfer is       บ
 บ  finished.  A quota of about 80 - 130 megs will do you fine if you're      บ
 บ  expecting some competition on the BBS.  When you download from your       บ
 บ  shell (using the 'sz' command at your prompt... 'sz *.zip') go and have   บ
 บ  a life.  Keep keep track of when the download should be done.  When you   บ
 บ  upload to a popular BBS you can expect that some of the files you         บ
 บ  leeched will already be on the BBS.  The key to getting on the top ten    บ
 บ  is for you to upload a lot of crap.  Upload anything any everything you   บ
 บ  can get your hands on.  Most system operators don't even bother to look   บ
 บ  at whats being uploaded (I've uploaded a Crayola Coloring Book once,      บ
 บ  blah, nuff said).  If your Internet provider is a bit expensive there is  บ
 บ  a second trick to getting files.  Just get a plain account at your ISP    บ
 บ  and PPP telnet to another server using a hacked account with a huge       บ
 บ  quota (Netcom seems to be the most popular) and fill up that shell.       บ
 บ  Then PPP leech it at your convience.  The transfer rates are a bit        บ
 บ  slower, but it's a lot cheaper.  I don't encourage this, but it works.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      BBS couriers usually have one advantage that FTP couriers don't       บ
 บ  have.  They get a ratio.  After about 6 months of uploading, you should   บ
 บ  have about 5 gigs of credit.  With that, you can just sit back and leech  บ
 บ  for eternity.  BBS couriering is a low stress and high profile job        บ
 บ  (depending on the BBS) that allows you to leech some fast stuff.  This    บ
 บ  is a good place for many couriers with a fast 33.6 modem and 200+ megs    บ
 บ  free on their HD to start at.  If you can't figure out how to find a      บ
 บ  person to apply for a group, your best bet would be to talk to the        บ
 บ  system operator of the BBS you're planning to courier for, or you could   บ
 บ  sit on IRC and beg for invites into a channel.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  IRC (Internet Relay Chat)                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Go into #Exceed, #M8leech, #THCfiles, or any of a zillion offer       บ
 บ  channel where you see those Lame-DCC and 31337-DCC guys.  Offering on     บ
 บ  IRC takes no talent and I do not even consider it real couriering.        บ
 บ  However, as IRC becomes more important to the scene and people flood      บ
 บ  onto IRC.  It might well become the new battle ground for groups when t3  บ
 บ  PPP connects become available in your own home 20 years from now.  A lot  บ
 บ  of groups have their IRC couriers spreading the group name and their      บ
 บ  presence among other lesser groups.  The better groups don't usually      บ
 บ  bother with offering since they focus on boards and sites.  DCC offering  บ
 บ  is a snap.  At your IRC prompt type '/xdcc offer' and hit enter.  Then    บ
 บ  give the file names you wanna offer and then put in a description.  When  บ
 บ  you want the channel to see your harvest of goodies type '/plist'.  I     บ
 บ  recommend the Venom.IRC and Phoenix.IRC scripts for offering.  Some       บ
 บ  people have been using the aDCC commands of LiCE script lately.  Use      บ
 บ  whatever script looks nice to you.  Set your minimum speed that you want  บ
 บ  to transfer at with '/xdcc minspeed'.  This way you can avoid some PPP    บ
 บ  whore leeching from you for hours at slow rates.  A minimum speed of 2    บ
 บ  to 3 kbs should be enough to keep the PPP and slow shell people out.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The only danger to IRC couriering is Chris Carter.  He is Narq        บ
 บ  extraordinaire.  He likes to hang out in #Exceed and the #WarezX          บ
 บ  channels.  Don't be surprised if you ISP admin tells you that the FBI is  บ
 บ  after you or something.  Chris Carter makes himself out to be a agent of  บ
 บ  some law organization, but in reality he is only a lamer who sits down    บ
 บ  at his computer and masturbates off of shareware.  Tell your IRC          บ
 บ  administrator that the man who mailed them is not an agent, he has no     บ
 บ  jurisdiction, and that as a paying customer you would appreciate some     บ
 บ  privacy.  Most administrators give you a slap on the wrist and don't      บ
 บ  care.  One of my former administrators actually gave me a higher quota    บ
 บ  cause he knew I was a trader (you'd be suprised how many ISPs have a      บ
 บ  secret warez drive).  Chris Carter has no power and he cannot do          บ
 บ  anything to you.  To avoid him you can use cracked shell accounts and     บ
 บ  offer from those.  I've been Chris Cartered about 7 times in my career    บ
 บ  and only one administrator freaked out.  If your administrator is         บ
 บ  actually suprised that pirates are the ones with the big HD quota, it's   บ
 บ  probabally time to find a new ISP.  IRC offering is an easy and simple    บ
 บ  way for small groups without FTP sites to move tagged files to the        บ
 บ  public.  It's not hard, and thus, has little glory in it.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I would like to thank Method Man who taught me everything about       บ
 บ  scripts I know.  He's such a freak that he even runs his own client.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  FTP (File Transfer Protocol)                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If you enjoy instant satisfaction and like having something about 5   บ
 บ  minutes before the rest of the scene, then FTP couriering is for you.     บ
 บ  FTP couriering is either easy or hard depending on the sites you have     บ
 บ  access to.  If you put RiSC against fATE it would be a slaughter because  บ
 บ  RiSC has a better FTP team and has some of the best sites on the planet.  บ
 บ  I would suggest that a FTP courier gain access to at least 2 to 3 super   บ
 บ  fast FTP sites and maybe 2 to 4 slower FTP sites where you can dominate.  บ
 บ  The trick is to get on as many FTP sites as you can at first and then     บ
 บ  work on getting onto the quality FTP sites.  For maximum output, you      บ
 บ  should have about 6 screens going at once and idling on the better        บ
 บ  sites.  Type 'ls' every minute so you don't time out.  Some FTP Couriers  บ
 บ  have scripts that do it automatically.  FTP couriering on fast sites can  บ
 บ  be stressful after sitting at your terminal for about 5 hours and         บ
 บ  looking at FTP sites to see if anything has come in the last few          บ
 บ  minutes.  A FTP courier must be on IRC and aware of group releases by     บ
 บ  paying attention to the sites all the time.  You have a window of about   บ
 บ  5 minutes or less before it hits the super fast FTP sites.  It takes      บ
 บ  about 20 minutes for it hits the slower sites.  After about 2 to 3 hours  บ
 บ  it's releasedd all over IRC and is offered in #exceed.  Software pirates  บ
 บ  have one of the greatist non-profit orginizations on the planet.  We can  บ
 บ  release something and it hits the whole world within 3 hours.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      FTP couriers usually use ncftp.  Type 'ncftp' at your unix prompt.    บ
 บ  Type 'open -u -p xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx xxxx' the -u means that it is not an     บ
 บ  anonymous login and the -p means that there is a port (if there isn't     บ
 บ  one, don't type -p).                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Once you get onto a FTP site, you will see that the directories are   บ
 บ  listed according to date.  If today was 11/06/95, I'd go to the 1106      บ
 บ  dir.  Inside that directory I would see a ton of warez.  Each release is  บ
 บ  in its own directory that either looks like 'lotus.notes.for.crap.blah'.  บ
 บ  You will usually see the full title or at least enough so you could       บ
 บ  figgure out what it is.  Some groups like fATE do lame junk like adding   บ
 บ  their groups name to the dir name 'fate-lamers.on.parade.full.cd.rip'.    บ
 บ  I don't encourage this since better FTP couriers frown on it as a form    บ
 บ  of lame bragging.  Most don't care what groups you are in.  They are      บ
 บ  only interested in the files.  To get the files onto your shell you type  บ
 บ  'mget *.zip'.  To upload your new goodies type 'mput filename*' to put    บ
 บ  multiple files from your shell to the FTP site.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Remeber to use ncftp, the mput and mget commands will not work if     บ
 บ  you type 'ftp xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx' in your shell.  When lamers type 'what'    บ
 บ  in the shell they can see the site numbers when you 'ftp                  บ
 บ  xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx' and they might try to hack you.  When running ncftp,     บ
 บ  all they will see is that little 'ncftp' flag.  FTP couriering is a       บ
 บ  quick way to get some warez and glory for your group.  Board couriers     บ
 บ  are a dime a dozen, a few good FTP couriers can make or break a group.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I would like to thank Ratz Blood and Weed who helped me when I was a  บ
 บ  little baby FTP courier.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Telnet                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are a few telnet boards now adays, but this might change in     บ
 บ  the future.  Only traders with experience and who are known usually get   บ
 บ  access to the good telnet boards.  The basic tool for telnet couriering   บ
 บ  is Ztel.  It allows you to upload using Zmodem.  To compile ztel.c on     บ
 บ  linux and/or Sun/OS, type 'gcc -o ztel ztel.c'.  If you have any          บ
 บ  problems just ask your ISP administrator (Ztel is is freeware).  Once     บ
 บ  your Ztel is compiled type '/home/path/ztel xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx xxxx'.    To  บ
 บ  upload, go through the normal upload procedure and wait for the Zmodem    บ
 บ  string.  Type 'control-a' then let go, then tap 'u'.  It will ask for     บ
 บ  file names or processes.  Type '*.zip' or whatever you want to upload.    บ
 บ  Ztel will download automatically if you want to leech some SNES games     บ
 บ  from Euro boards.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Here's where it gets a bit tricky.  To use screen and ztel together   บ
 บ  (screen allows you to multitask in your shell) you must type this when    บ
 บ  you initialize your screen 'screen -e ^Tt'.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I would like to thank Superior Force and Fortune for helping me       บ
 บ  learn how to use Ztel and screen together.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Author  : Instant Rage                                                  บ
 บ    Subject : Napalm FUCKS Up..                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Lately, it seems that Napalm is dominating the games scene, with      บ
 บ  their pure abundance of releases, not to mention the speed at which they  บ
 บ  release them.  There is one problem though, and we see it almost every    บ
 บ  time there is a Napalm release.  Napalm can't release a single thing      บ
 บ  without some kind of problem with the game.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      We all know about Napalm's little problem, and we have all            บ
 บ  complained about it at one time or another, but this article is not to    บ
 บ  complain about Napalm, it's to congratulate them.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Napalm has gotten so good at fixing problems, it seems that there is  บ
 บ  a seperate 'fix' for every game they release.  Napalm is such an          บ
 บ  EXTREMELY FAST releasing group, they almost always miss a problem with    บ
 บ  the game the first time round.  I criticized them for this before, and    บ
 บ  now they have perfected the art of releasing.  In other words, they       บ
 บ  still release the game fast, and THEN they fix it, once everyone has it.  บ
 บ  It's a great strategy, and because of it, you see Napalm outrunning       บ
 บ  vetran groups such as Razor 1911 and Hybrid through sheer SPEED.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What's more, it seems that lately, Napalm has gotten good at          บ
 บ  covering ass, big time.  You see, in the not so long ago release of       บ
 บ  Lemmings Paintball, which was released by Hybrid, there was a CD check    บ
 บ  that for some reason Hybrid failed to find.  The most surprising part     บ
 บ  though, was that Napalm almost instantly released a fix for Hybrid's      บ
 บ  mess, just like they do for their own releases.  If you ask me, Napalm    บ
 บ  is trying to prove themselves, and they are doing a VERY good job, don't  บ
 บ  you think?                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Author  : Kang                                                          บ
 บ    Subject : Macintosh Takeover???                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      On Wednesday, May 22, channel #Warez666 was taken over.  It looked    บ
 บ  like a pretty nice takeover from what I could see.  The takeover was      บ
 บ  planned beforehand with extreme care.  The people who took over the       บ
 บ  channel setup bots which changed handles every 5 seconds, in order to     บ
 บ  avoid being flooded.  What made it even more strange was that these       บ
 บ  people who took over the channel have never before been seen in the       บ
 บ  warez scene.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Beware, if you run a channel for a group or for private use, you      บ
 บ  might be the next one to feel their takeover wrath.  The following is     บ
 บ  a series of log files from the scene of the takeover :                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I spoke with Spawn666 who is a fellow THC (The Hardened Criminals)    บ
 บ  member and a #Warez666 operator.  I was informed that the old #Warez666   บ
 บ  operators were not planning to take back the channel.  They were just     บ
 บ  idling, waiting for the new operators to make a mistake.  An hour after   บ
 บ  the take over, the new operators started to ping timeout one after the    บ
 บ  other.  The new operators kicked nearly everyone out of the channel and   บ
 บ  set it to +i.  When the bot ping timed out, the old operators flooded     บ
 บ  the others off and took the channel.  It was only a matter of hours       บ
 บ  before the channel was taken back.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You might say, "Who cares?  It's like a fly on an elephants ass."     บ
 บ  But the point is that no matter how elite you may be, everyone screws up  บ
 บ  sometimes.  None of the #Warez666 ops wanted to talk after the fact.      บ
 บ  The Trader, from fATE (Fast Action Trade Exchange), informed me later     บ
 บ  that day that the takeover was due to Pickels having been spoofed by a    บ
 บ  Macintosh user.  #Warez666 is a good channel once more, owned by IBM      บ
 บ  elites.                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Author  : Tuxedo Mask                                                   บ
 บ    Subject : Tai Pan *BUSTED*                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The following is an excerpt from the letter spread by the late Tai Pan    บ
 บ  on May 19, 1996 :                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As of today my role as a courier for ROR (Release on Rampage), RTS    บ
 บ  (Request to Send), and MTY (Mortality) has been cut short.  Since         บ
 บ  February, I have been making long distance calls using extrapolated       บ
 บ  credit card numbers (fake).  In May, AT&T finally caught on and           บ
 บ  backbilled me for about $1000.  My parents were not too pleased with      บ
 บ  this and since it was the second time I was caught, decided to revoke my  บ
 บ  online access.  My data line, Internet provider, CompuServe account, and  บ
 บ  shell account have all been cancelled and my modem will be taken out of   บ
 บ  my computer in 3 hours.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The moral of this story is DON'T CARD!  Since everyone knows that     บ
 บ  option is ridiculous at least be careful.  But seriously, try and trade   บ
 บ  (like Stingray6) from your office.  They pick up the bill and it's        บ
 บ  LEGAL.  It has been fun everyone!  I'll be around on TAR, PC, and         บ
 บ  666-KILL for those who want to leave me a message.  However, I won't      บ
 บ  trade anymore unless I can find a way to do it outside my house.  I       บ
 บ  shall return to the scene in about a year when I'm in college.  So until  บ
 บ  then, keep on trading and keep the scene alive!                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Tai Pan                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  admired by us all.. you just keep coming back bust after bust like a      บ
 บ  pirate energizer bunny.  See you next year!                               บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Tuxedo Mask                                                   บ
 บ    Subject : DVD (Digital Video Discs)                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      DVD players will make their debuts as movie playback machines and     บ
 บ  recordable DVD-ROM drives for PCs.  A technology as new as DVD is         บ
 บ  typically too expensive to be of interest to console manufacturers such   บ
 บ  as Nintendo and Sega, but all the major PC manufacturers are watching     บ
 บ  DVD's approach with varying degrees of interest.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Support for DVD from the dedicated game machine manufacturers,        บ
 บ  however, is not entirely enthusiastic, and is sure to change the warez    บ
 บ  scene in the future.  Shortly after the DVD movie player hits the         บ
 บ  market, the first DVD-ROM drives will ship for the PC.  Initially, these  บ
 บ  drives are expected to retail for somewhere between $400 and $600.  With  บ
 บ  a storage capacity of 4.7 gigabytes (versus CD-ROMs which hold 0.65       บ
 บ  gigabytes) and vastly increased data transfer rates, the DVD-ROM will     บ
 บ  offer developers the chance to produce titles with broadcast-quality      บ
 บ  video and surround-sound audio.  In addition to the more immersive sound  บ
 บ  and video, the increased storage capacity will enable the developers to   บ
 บ  place more levels and/or more complex databases in their titles.  As      บ
 บ  titles released onto the market use the DVD as a standard format, we      บ
 บ  will be sure to see meggage of the releases by warez groups increase in   บ
 บ  size.  Instead of 30 disk releases, we might be in wait for 300 disk      บ
 บ  releases.  However, we need not fear, as technology for storage           บ
 บ  capacities increase, so will the technology for fiber optic connections,  บ
 บ  thus increasing transfer speeds.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Like CD-ROM and CD-dependent game machines, there will be no real     บ
 บ  difference in the physical make-up between the DVD-ROM drives available   บ
 บ  for the PCs, and DVD-ROM drives will eventually become part of dedicated  บ
 บ  game machines.  When will DVD game machines appear?  In general, it       บ
 บ  seems that the gaming manufacturers are content to wait on the sidelines  บ
 บ  for now and to let the folks on the PC side struggle with early           บ
 บ  compatibility and pricing issues.  As DVD-ROM drives become available to  บ
 บ  a larger audience, we are sure to see DVD-ROM pirate libraries that       บ
 บ  would be able to hold close to a 500 to 800 games.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Last, but not least, is the possibility of a DVD audio disc.  The     บ
 บ  majority of current audio CDs, like many games on CD, do not use the      บ
 บ  entire space on their current media, and so the demand for DVD audio      บ
 บ  discs is almost nonexistent.  The opportunity exists, however, to do      บ
 บ  more with audio DVD, especially if it is compatible with the recordable   บ
 บ  DVD-ROM drive.  If those capabilities come to fruition, people will be    บ
 บ  able to record hours of digital audio onto a disc at their discretion.    บ
 บ  In that sense, the DVD audio and DVD-ROM would elevate the disc medium    บ
 บ  to a place that the CD never evolved to en masse : serving as mass        บ
 บ  storage medium.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So far, the only DVD spec that has been released is one general and   บ
 บ  vague outline for both the DVD movie player and DVD-ROM drive.  Although  บ
 บ  it is somewhat vague, the spec does revel the basic parameters and        บ
 บ  technologies of DVD.  It's 4.7 gigabytes storage capacity is certainly a  บ
 บ  considerable improvement over the 0.65 of CD-ROMS, as is its 4.69         บ
 บ  megabits-per-second average transfer rate (a single speed CD-ROM player   บ
 บ  reads datat at a rate of just 0.15 megabits-per-second).  This            บ
 บ  improvement in performance, however, will require additional processing   บ
 บ  muscle in the host machine to handle all the data.  Consumer DVD movie    บ
 บ  players will need to include MPEG2 and AC3 audio decoding solutions, and  บ
 บ  it is anticipated that nothing short of a Pentium 166 MHz will make full  บ
 บ  use of a DVD-ROM player for a PC.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Perhaps DVD's main advantage will be in the fact that the option      บ
 บ  exists to make the discs recordable.  Some companies have said that they  บ
 บ  are working to make their first DVD-ROM drives off the production line    บ
 บ  recordable.  And erasable DVD-ROMs, if they aren't shipped initially,     บ
 บ  are expected to ship on an OEM (Original Equipment Manufacture) basis     บ
 บ  soon after.  Another issue to be ironed out is whether or not the discs   บ
 บ  will be able to store data on just one side or both sides of the disc.    บ
 บ  In the original specs, the discs were planned to be two sided.  However,  บ
 บ  the two-sided configuration was being considered only as "possible".      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Of course, the whole issue of price is perhaps the major hurdle       บ
 บ  still to be negotiated by those wishing to rush DVD to the market.  And   บ
 บ  once it does hit the market, we can see that BBSes with the DVD           บ
 บ  technology will be able to offer a far greater library of downloads than  บ
 บ  the BBSes which do not yet have DVD.  Whatever the price, DVD is          บ
 บ  guaranteed to change the face of the warez scene.  Whatever the specs of  บ
 บ  the DVD, no one really knows whether it will be the warez scene killer,   บ
 บ  or a new device that will revolutionize the warez scene.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ


                         ฐ
    ฿฿        ฐ  ฿     ฿฿฿ฐ                      ฐ฿฿฿
     ฿ ฿  ฿฿฿  ฿฿฿   ฿    ฿  r c n          ฿฿ ฿฿
   ฿ ฐ฿  ฿               ฿   ฿ฐ   ฿
 ฐ ฐฐ ฐ ฿฿ฐ ฐ฿ ฿฿ ฐ  ฿฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐ  ฿ฐฐฐฐฐฐ ฐฐฐ
        ฿        ฐ฿฿฿฿฿฿   ฿฿       ฿฿        
                              ฐ฿฿฿฿฿    ฿฿ฐ฿฿฿฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป

 บ    Author  : Instant Rage                                                  บ
 บ    Subject : Console Warez                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      For many years, PC users have strived to run software on their        บ
 บ  computer that wasn't ever meant to be run; software from other            บ
 บ  platforms.  You may have seen several of these "emulators", in which you  บ
 บ  can play your favorite Super NES game in a little window on your          บ
 บ  desktop.  Because you are running something foreign on your computer,     บ
 บ  many things must be given up, such as sound effects, music, and your      บ
 บ  favorite joypad.  Why do we want to play them then?  Maybe we just miss   บ
 บ  a favorite game we had, or maybe we just want to prove that it can be     บ
 บ  done, but it seems kind of stupid when you think about it, doesn't it?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Even though the emulators that run console warez is fairly new, the   บ
 บ  history of console warez is a long one.  You see, a long time ago, if     บ
 บ  you wanted to run a copied Super NES, or Gameboy game, you needed an      บ
 บ  actual console to run them (hence the name), and a "cartridge drive"      บ
 บ  that accepted Super NES or Gameboy cartridges.  At one point in time,     บ
 บ  this was such a popular thing, there were actually groups devoted to      บ
 บ  bringing in console warez, just as there are groups that bring in new PC  บ
 บ  software everyday.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Even still, you have to wonder why they did all this.  After all, we  บ
 บ  all have a PC, and there are great games released everyday that make      บ
 บ  some Super NES games blow mega farts.  Now, with emulators that actually  บ
 บ  work, the fad to play them is even greater, and you can pick up a 'game   บ
 บ  pack' just about every month.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      For those of you who love to piss with emulators, here is some        บ
 บ  information to get you going.  The only working Super NES emulator for    บ
 บ  PC is for Windows 95, and it was originally released in Japanese or some  บ
 บ  other funky language, but there are numerous versions that have been      บ
 บ  translated so that they are understandable.  The version that works       บ
 บ  supports only the .SFC extension (Super FamiCom).  Beware that there are  บ
 บ  very many other types of Super NES image files (for the console drives),  บ
 บ  and that if you come across one (SMC, SNS, etc.) you should find          บ
 บ  yourself a program called CTOOL that will convert the file to the one     บ
 บ  you need.  If you ever encounter a Super NES game broken down like this   บ
 บ  'kinstnct.1, kinstnct.2, etc.', CTOOL will also combine these files so    บ
 บ  that they will become one 'kinstnct.sfc'.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There is a Gameboy emulator for both Windows 95 and DOS, both of      บ
 บ  which work quite well (much more stable then the Super NES emulator),     บ
 บ  and they both support the only extension I know of (.GB).  So you should  บ
 บ  have no problem playing Wario Land in black and white.. or should you?    บ
 บ  You still won't get any sound, and chances are, your game will freeze in  บ
 บ  the middle, right when you are just getting into it.  It doesn't seem     บ
 บ  worth it, but it doesn't stop you from trying.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Let's all play Lameboy games on a $3000 computer!  Hooray!            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ฐฐฐ ฿   ฿ฐ ฐ ฿ ฐฐฐ฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐฐฐ  ฿ ฐ ฐฐฐฐ ฐฐ

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the six best games release groups in the scene.  บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 04/25/96 -> 05/01/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the six best games release groups in the scene.  บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the six best games release groups in the scene.  บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 05/09/96 -> 05/15/96            ณ  บ

                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the six best games release groups in the scene.  บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 05/16/96 -> 05/22/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the six best utils release groups in the scene.  บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 04/25/96 -> 05/01/96            ณ  บ
