 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the six best utils release groups in the scene.  บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 05/02/96 -> 05/08/96            ณ  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the six best utils release groups in the scene.  บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ

                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the six best utils release groups in the scene.  บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Welcome to Dear Road Rebel!  This is going to be YOUR column that is  บ
 บ  a cross between Dear Abby and Dave Berry.  The most important part of     บ
 บ  this is YOUR participation.  If you have ever had a question about the    บ
 บ  scene or just a comment, here's the place!  Have you ever wanted to know  บ
 บ  why some people do this or that?  ASK!  I would love to take it to the    บ
 บ  extreme for you and we will be happy to research it!  I hope you have as  บ
 บ  much fun with this as I will!  Remember, this is YOUR column!             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Road Rebel,                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The BBS scene pimped on the Internet scene.  It was so much more      บ
 บ  interesting to be in!  I mean getting stuff around in 0-2 day was HARD!   บ
 บ  It took skilled couriers.  I think the Internet ruined everything.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Koon Dog                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Koon Dog,                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I think you're very right, the BBS scene involved much more skill.    บ
 บ  People would spend countless hours logging onto boards around the world   บ
 บ  to get new releases so they could put everything around the world and     บ
 บ  get all the releases out.  But why do you think the Internet ruined       บ
 บ  EVERYTHING?  I think it raised the competition that much higher.  Now     บ
 บ  people really have to try hard to get places before others do.  When the  บ
 บ  Internet wasn't around, the competition was not to get stuff around       บ
 บ  faster than anybody else, but to get stuff around at all.  Now, we have   บ
 บ  so many great couriers and they all try to push the same stuff to the     บ
 บ  same place, and people lose by mere seconds.  I think that makes things   บ
 บ  that much harder.  But of course, "it is not who does it first, it's who  บ
 บ  does it right," and it could quite easily be said that much of today's    บ
 บ  scene is filled with bad releases that don't work.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Road Rebel                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Road Rebel,                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ          The Internet has fixed some things and fucked up other things.    บ
 บ  Couriers are having a ball now trying to do things before others.         บ
 บ  However, like you say, there are some new problems.  Many boards are      บ
 บ  getting partial releases and that doesn't help anybody.  It makes the     บ
 บ  courier look bad and then makes the group look stupid.  Ultimately, it    บ
 บ  lowers the quality of the board.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Zero Prime                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Reader,                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I think you bring out an interesting point.  The scene is currently   บ
 บ  in a transition regarding the Internet and the BBS scene.  The Internet,  บ
 บ  I think, will end up prevailing, but while we're making this transition   บ
 บ  from BBS to Internet, the two are clashing.  We're going from one         บ
 บ  resource that can push a meg per second, to a resource that pushes no     บ
 บ  more than 3k per second.  That's a huge bottleneck, and one that will be  บ
 บ  resolved as soon as we start getting BBSs running on private T1's and     บ
 บ  Cable modems.  Until then, the bottleneck will still slow us down.  As    บ
 บ  soon as the transition is complete, the scene will breathe a fresher      บ
 บ  air.                                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Road Rebel                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Topic For Next Week : Week Old Group                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ          As always, we see about three new groups a week, and about three  บ
 บ  more die every week.  However, none of these groups grow beyond 2 or 3    บ
 บ  releases.  Every once in a while, if we're lucky, the group ends up       บ
 บ  releasing on a regular basis.  Sounds like a winner, right?  Wrong.       บ
 บ  Most often, the group's releases don't work, are uncracked, or even       บ
 บ  incomplete.  One would think, in theory, that new groups can't hurt       บ
 บ  anything.  Sure, there could be too many of them, and they take up time,  บ
 บ  but if they release, they're helping the scene.  However, this is hardly  บ
 บ  the case.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The situation has become so bad that now, when one finds a release    บ
 บ  that he wants, he must check twice to see what group released it.         บ
 บ  Often, if the group is not a megafigure such as DOD or PWA, Razor or      บ
 บ  Dynamix, he won't even download it, for fear of wasting an hour of his    บ
 บ  time just to find that what he downloaded doesn't even work.  So, what's  บ
 บ  the alternative for the hopefuls to get big in the scene?  What do you    บ
 บ  think these small groups are doing to the scene as a whole?  Do you       บ
 บ  think they benefit it, or inhibit its success?  Do you think their        บ
 บ  releases, even though small in number, are worth downloading?  Do you     บ
 บ  trust them?  Write back and tell us what you think!                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In an effort to stop software piracy on the Internet, I have been     บ
 บ  monitoring various groups of users on the Internet Relay Chat network.    บ
 บ  This medium of communication has become very popular with "warez"         บ
 บ  pirates who exchange commercial software illegally.  On the IRC network,  บ
 บ  groups of people come together to use sophisticated methods to            บ
 บ  distribute commercial software to literally thousands of users.  With     บ
 บ  such large scale distribution methods, the software industry is losing    บ
 บ  millions of dollars.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I have no direct evidence to show you that this user is               บ
 บ  participating in illegal activities.  But I can direct you to where       บ
 บ  evidence can be found.  If you are permitted to do so, I suggest that     บ
 บ  you take a brief scan of the user's home-directory and check for any      บ
 บ  suspicious files.  If you cannot do this, I recommend that you keep a     บ
 บ  close eye on this user and watch for any unusual activities.  Please      บ
 บ  take whatever action is appropriate in dealing with these matters as      บ
 บ  stated in your organization's Internet Policy Agreement or Network        บ
 บ  Etiquette Policy.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Thank you for taking the time to read through this message.  And      บ
 บ  thank you for any assistance you can give to help resolve this matter.    บ
 บ  Your time and help is greatly appreciated and I give you my full          บ
 บ  gratitude.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                        Thanks again,                       บ
 บ                                        Chris Carter                        บ
 บ                                        International Internet Association  บ
 บ                                        chrisc@free.org                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ      I have found a user in your Internet domain who plays a large role    บ
 บ  in the distribution of copyrighted software on the Internet.  This user   บ
 บ  uses the nickname "BN" and uses the account "x@x.x.fi.".  He/she is a     บ
 บ  member of an underground group called "Rapier."  This group is dedicated  บ
 บ  to the transfer of illegal commerical software to a large audience of     บ
 บ  users on the Internet.  They use the most efficient and fastest methods   บ
 บ  possible.                                                                 บ
 บ                                        Thanks again,                       บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I believe this user, Chris Carter, is violating numerous laws, to     บ
 บ  include guidelines set forth by the Electronic Frontier Foundation        บ
 บ  (EFF).  His means of monitoring are clearly illegal in the United         บ
 บ  States.  He is known to use hacked accounts, send false mail, hide his    บ
 บ  address, monitor channels in "IRC" through stealth modes - his presence   บ
 บ  not visible to users of the channels.  He is also making great            บ
 บ  accusations with no evidence causing undue harassment and libel.  Undue   บ
 บ  conflict between user and administrator and possibly resulting in the     บ
 บ  loss of accounts, if not involvement by state/local/federal authorities.  บ
 บ  Chris Carter's tactics seem to be strategic and premeditative in nature,  บ
 บ  a direct attack on the reputation of whomever he chooses to harass.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It is encouraged that the unethical and unlawful behavior of Chris    บ
 บ  Carter be stopped, to protect privacy, freedom of speech, reputations of  บ
 บ  the innocent and prevent him from abusing any other computer systems      บ
 บ  through subversive and/or illegal "hacking" methods.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Chris Carter certainly gets around.  Upon mention of his name, many   บ
 บ  people have spoken out in outrage at his actions and methods. This        บ
 บ  e-mail is a collective result of concerned citizens in both the United    บ
 บ  States and abroad.  To my knowledge, there are seven other instances of   บ
 บ  such accusations sent via e-mail with no support.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Upon contact, a system administrator from the first provider has      บ
 บ  stated that they have checked the files of the user in question,          บ
 บ  permissible by a written legal form signed by the account purchaser, and  บ
 บ  have not found a single thing of illegal nature.  Why is this violation   บ
 บ  of privacy necessary due to the likes of Mr. Carter, who does not seem    บ
 บ  to respect the rights of innocent people?  One must wonder whether        บ
 บ  Carter's basis for these accusing messages has anything to do with the    บ
 บ  reason of "software piracy" as Carter states.  If so, his observations    บ
 บ  are error-prone.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The second provider involved has not commented.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Thank you for your time and, hopefully, support.  Chris Carter is a   บ
 บ  criminal by any standards and must be dealt with by legal means before    บ
 บ  spreading more harm among the Internet community.                         บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Instant Rage                                                  บ
 บ    Subject : M'name is Chicken, Rebel Chicken.  People call me...          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The other day, I was sitting in the can of a public restroom, and     บ
 บ  among the scribbles on the wall, I noticed something that meant           บ
 บ  something to me.  Somebody had etched the words "PiL 96 !!" on the wall   บ
 บ  with a black marker while taking a shit.  I sat there and thought, and    บ
 บ  thought.. then I wondered if these were actually the scribbles of a       บ
 บ  member of Pirates in Legion, the present but forgotten utils group.  Or   บ
 บ  I suppose it could have been a VERY happy fan, but who knows.  All that   บ
 บ  thinking encouraged me to stay on the can and think some more.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      All this thinking led me to think about the importance of group       บ
 บ  names.  When thoughts come about a group like fATE, do you think of the   บ
 บ  meaning behind it?  Somebody put a lot of thought into that name (maybe   บ
 บ  they were on the can like me), and it brings importance to the group.     บ
 บ  The word fATE alone can make you think about alot of things, but the      บ
 บ  underlying meaning is still "Fast Action Trade Exchange".                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Other names that we know of, such as PWA, or even COPS, makes one     บ
 บ  laugh when we think of the meaning.  I know I'm not the only one who      บ
 บ  thinks Pirates with Attitudes is just a little cheezzzy, let alone        บ
 บ  Couriers of Pirated Software.  But we look and we laugh, after all, we    บ
 บ  can't let the scene get too serious now, can we?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A few more minutes of shitting led me to think about the importance   บ
 บ  of handles.  There are some funny names of groups out there, and I        บ
 บ  realzied that could extend outside the spectrum of mere group names.      บ
 บ  Many handles of the people in the scene are equally ridiculous.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      For example, if you can recall the handle of Fan Fan La Tulipe, the   บ
 บ  late President of TDU-JAM!, or our very own RCN editor, Rebel Chicken.    บ
 บ  Both these names are extremely ridiculous, but none the less, it's not    บ
 บ  the name that really matters, it's what's backed by it.  You could call   บ
 บ  yourself ABC or 123 if you really wanted to, and it wouldn't make a       บ
 บ  difference, it's not your handle that's important, the important matter   บ
 บ  is the substance that backs it up.  And the same can be said for groups,  บ
 บ  you could start a group called RWN, Raisins with Nuts, but if that group  บ
 บ  releases consistent quality or couriers in a fashion revolutionizing to   บ
 บ  the scene, then that group will receive the recognition and respect it    บ
 บ  deserves regardless of its cheezzzy name.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : 5 Minutes                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The bell rings.  I am faster than the bell, I had packed my bag 20    บ
 บ  seconds prior.  As I was walking toward my next class, I couldn't help    บ
 บ  but notice that to my left was Emily, I think of her as this really       บ
 บ  stupid blonde girl, and Hitex thinks of her as "pimple face".             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Oh God, please tell me Emily doesn't see me, I don't feel like        บ
 บ  talking to anyone right now, especially not her.  May be I can just       บ
 บ  mingle to the right of the hallway and hide behind some freshman.  The    บ
 บ  day is not going well.  The stupid blonde girl greets me and starts       บ
 บ  small talk.  I am extremely agitated and I wish that she'd just leave me  บ
 บ  alone.  I can see that she starts her conversations the same way every    บ
 บ  single time, no matter who she's talking to.  In fact, everyone from my   บ
 บ  high school talks the same.  Everyone says the same thing, the same way,  บ
 บ  and by far, I am as guilty of that as anyone else.  I can read their      บ
 บ  minds and I perceive that what they say and what they feel are as         บ
 บ  different as night and day.  I show interest in what she says.  I smile.  บ
 บ  I nod my head.  I smile again, and I wish to myself that she would shut   บ
 บ  up.                                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now I'm really in trouble,  our conversation has superseded the       บ
 บ  usual "How are you doing" and the "I'm doing great" bullshit, and she's   บ
 บ  going out of her routine small talk.  She asks me a question.  Even       บ
 บ  though I have no idea what her question is, I try my best to reply.  I    บ
 บ  give her the no fuss answer, "Wow, that's cool."                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I see her lips move up and down again, but I have no idea what the    บ
 บ  hell she's saying.  She pauses and smiles.  I see her smile and so I      บ
 บ  smile back, and I assume that it is time for me to reply, so I say to     บ
 บ  her, "Wow, that is REALLY REALLY cool."                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Suddenly, I grow very confused.  I start asking myself questions I    บ
 บ  have never even thought of before.  I know that these questions I am      บ
 บ  asking myself have always been part of me, but it is only now that I am   บ
 บ  allowing them to surface.  I ponder.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Why can't she just be herself?  I know she is not very fond of me.    บ
 บ  Why is she acting like she's my friend.  I don't even know her that       บ
 บ  well; the only reason link I have to her is that I sit next to her in my  บ
 บ  English IV class, I hardly doubt that's a basis for friendship.  Is she   บ
 บ  acting nice because it's othe cool thing to do?"  And, why can't she      บ
 บ  stop talking, she is becoming very annoying.  She asks me another         บ
 บ  question, this time, I don't know what to do.  To think that I used to    บ
 บ  want to go out with her, yuck.. what the hell was I thinking?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A part of me speaks, the part of me that stems from archaic roots     บ
 บ  takes over.  I will have to sacrifice dearly, but today, I will let my    บ
 บ  dark side take over.  In a matter of 20 seconds, I will destroy the       บ
 บ  "nice guy" image I had worked so hard building up these last 4 years.  I  บ
 บ  was good at deceiving people, I got them all to think that I was a "nice  บ
 บ  guy".  Not this time though, I don't really care anymore.  I choose to    บ
 บ  come out of the closet, so to speak, I'm going to just be myself.  I say  บ
 บ  to her in my own tone, without smiling, "What the fuck is wrong with      บ
 บ  you?  Can't you tell that I have absolutely no fucking interest in what   บ
 บ  you're saying to me?"  I said it really loud, and nearly everyone in the  บ
 บ  hallway stops to look at me.  I feel very embarrassed, but I don't care,  บ
 บ  I am having fun.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Unfortunately, one of the people who hears me yell at the stupid      บ
 บ  blonde girl, was the Principal.  The Principal rushes to me and puts his  บ
 บ  hand on my back.  He asks me why I was acting so agitated, and asks me    บ
 บ  whether or not I needed to go to the nurse's office.  The Principal must  บ
 บ  think I'm mentally unstable.  Well, I'm NOT crazy, I'm just elite.  I     บ
 บ  tell him that I am not crazy, and that I was merely acting natural, I     บ
 บ  couldn't take it anymore.  The bitch was too annoying, I only did that    บ
 บ  which was necessary to prevent mental collapse.  I haven't been myself    บ
 บ  for nearly 4 years now.  I don't want to fall into that trap again, like  บ
 บ  before, I didn't want to end my conversation without showing her who I    บ
 บ  really was.  I don't regret any of what I did.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The Principal slaps on my back a pink sheet.  On that pink sheet, I   บ
 บ  read, "Two hours detention."  I shrug and I start walking back toward my  บ
 บ  next class, I feel free, free again, free at last, and once again, I      บ
 บ  here a voice saying, "I don't regret any of what I did."                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
